add_namespace = WORLD
add_namespace = novel #for althist novels

#Aleutians Crisis
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.70
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.70" }
	title = WORLD.70.t
	desc = WORLD.70.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_USA_aleutians_crisis

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.70.a #USA
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.70.b #Japan
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = WORLD.70.c #Germany
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.70.d #rest of the world, except Mexico
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = JAP
				tag = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #The Boer War
	id = WORLD.35
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.35" }
	title = WORLD.35.t
	desc = WORLD.35.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_SAF_artillery

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.35.a
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BOR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.35.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GRO
				original_tag = COG
				original_tag = ANG
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_SOUTH_AFRICAN_WAR }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.35.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = SAF
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_SOUTH_AFRICAN_WAR }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.35.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = BOR
				original_tag = COG
				original_tag = ANG
				original_tag = SAF
				original_tag = GRO
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_SOUTH_AFRICAN_WAR }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {
			tag = IBR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.b #non far-right countries
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = progressivism
				has_government = liberalism
				has_government = liberal_conservatism
				has_government = conservatism
				has_government = paternalism
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.c #far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
				tag = MEX
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = despotism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = ultranationalism
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.d #Mexico
		trigger = {
			tag = MEX
		}
	}
}

		}

		set_country_flag = IBR_decisions_foreign
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = IBR_Francisco_Franco
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { IBR_caudillo_correct_var = 1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IBRIberiaStability
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_sub_stability_small_tt

		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_pp_foreign_get_tt

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = IBR.31051
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = ITA
				original_tag = IBR
			}
		}
	}

news_event = { #Falangists Seize Power in Iberia
	id = WORLD.1500
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.1500" }
	title = WORLD.1500.t
	desc = WORLD.1500.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_IBR_armada_coup

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.a #iberia
		trigger = {
			tag = IBR
		}
		TNO_Country_Closing_Screen_Show = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.b #non far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = progressivism
				has_government = liberalism
				has_government = liberal_conservatism
				has_government = conservatism
				has_government = paternalism
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.c #far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = despotism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = ultranationalism
			}

		}
	}
}

				set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_BRITISH_REUNIFICATION_MAUDLING }

				TNO_fire_super_event = yes
			}
			else_if = {

		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_HUTTIG_COLLAPSE }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { FIN_party_pops^8 = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { FIN_party_pops^9 = 3 }
		}
	}
}

	title = WORLD_GRE.8.t

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # For a new Greece!
		name = WORLD_GRE.8.a
		trigger = {
			tag = GRE
		}
	}

	option = { # Prepare a response!
		name = WORLD_GRE.8.b
		trigger = {
			tag = ITA
		}
	}

	option = { # who gives a shit?
		name = WORLD_GRE.8.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = ITA
				tag = GRE
			}
		}
	}
}
